### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 93 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Context: Jennifer bought a box of Crunchy Grain cereal. The nutrition facts on the box state that a serving size of the cereal is $\frac{3}{4}$ cup and provides 210 calories, 50 of which are calories from fat. In addition, each serving of the cereal provides 180 milligrams of potassium, which is $5 \%$ of the daily allowance for adults.
Question: On Tuesday, Jennifer will mix Crunchy Grain cereal with Super Grain cereal for her breakfast. Super Grain cereal provides 240 calories per cup. If the total number of calories in one cup of Jennifer's mixture is 270, how much Super Grain cereal is in one cup of the mixture?
Choices:
  A: $\frac{1}{8} \operatorname{cup}$
  B: $\frac{1}{4} \operatorname{cup}$
  C: $\frac{1}{3} \operatorname{cup}$
  D: $\frac{1}{2} \operatorname{cup}$
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume that Jennifer mixes $x$ cups of Super Grain cereal with $\frac{3}{4}-x$ cups of Crunchy Grain cereal.
  The total number of calories in the mixture is the sum of the calories from each cereal.
  We know that Crunchy Grain cereal provides 210 calories per $\frac{3}{4}$ cup, which is equivalent to 280 calories per cup.
  We also know that the total number of calories in one cup of the mixture is 270.
  Therefore, we can write the following equation:
  $$
  280 \left(\frac{3}{4}-x\right)+240 x=270
  $$
  Solving for $x$, we get:
  $$
  x=\frac{1}{3}
  $$
  Therefore, Jennifer mixes $\frac{1}{3}$ cup of Super Grain cereal with $\frac{3}{4}-\frac{1}{3}=\frac{1}{2}$ cup of Crunchy Grain cereal.
  The answer is $\frac{1}{3}$ cup.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Let's assume that Jennifer mixes $x$ cups of Super Grain cereal with $\frac{3}{4}-x$ cups of Crunchy Grain cereal.
  The total calories in one cup of the mixture is 270.
  The total calories in one cup of Super Grain cereal is 240.
  Therefore, the total calories in one cup of Crunchy Grain cereal is $\frac{210}{\frac{3}{4}}=280$.

  $$
  240x+280\left(\frac{3}{4}-x\right)=270
  $$

  $$
  x=\frac{1}{3}

  Let's subtract the calories from Crunchy Grain cereal from the total number of calories to get the calories from Super Grain cereal.
  Calories from Super Grain cereal = Total calories - Calories from Crunchy Grain cereal
  Calories from Super Grain cereal = 270 - 280 = -10

- The equation is $240x + 210\left(\frac{3}{4}\right) = 270(x + \frac{3}{4})$.
- Solving for $x$ gives $x = \frac{1}{3}$.
- Therefore, Jennifer uses $\frac{1}{3}$ cup of Super Grain cereal in one cup of the mixture.
- The answer is C: $\frac{1}{3} \operatorname{cup}$.

Question: $$h=-16 t^{2}+v t+k$$The equation above gives the height $h$, in feet, of a ball $t$ seconds after it is thrown straight up with an initial speed of $v$ feet per second from a height of $k$ feet. Which of the following gives $v$ in terms of $h, t$, and $k$ ?
Choices:
  A: $v=h+k-16 t$
  B: $v=\frac{h-k+16}{t}$
  C: $v=\frac{h+k}{t}-16 t$
  D: $v=\frac{h-k}{t}+16 t$
Response 0:
Thought:
  The equation given is $h=-16 t^{2}+v t+k$.
  We need to isolate $v$.
  We can do this by adding $16t^2$ to both sides of the equation.
  This gives us $16t^2+h=vt+k$.
  We can then subtract $k$ from both sides of the equation.
  This gives us $16t^2+h-k=vt$.
  Finally, we can divide both sides of the equation by $t$.
  This gives us $v=\frac{16t^2+h-k}{t}$.
  Therefore, the answer is D: $v=\frac{h-k}{t}+16 t$.
Action: Answer("D")

  A: $3 x+2 y=6$
  B: $3 x+4 y=6$
  C: $2 x+4 y=6$
  D: $2 x+6 y=3$

The equation of a line perpendicular to another line has a slope that is the negative reciprocal of the slope of the original line.
The given equation can be rewritten in slope-intercept form as $y=\frac{2}{3}x+2$.
The negative reciprocal of $\frac{2}{3}$ is $-\frac{3}{2}$.
Therefore, we need to find an equation with a slope of $-\frac{3}{2}$.
The slope of each equation can be found by rearranging it into slope-intercept form.
The equation with a slope of $-\frac{3}{2}$ is $3x+2y=6$.
Therefore, the answer is A: $3x+2y=6$.

Question: The Downtown Business Association (DBA) in a certain city plans to increase its membership by a total of $n$ businesses per year. There were $b$ businesses in the DBA at the beginning of this year. Which function best models the total number of businesses, $y$, the DBA plans to have as members $x$ years from now?
Choices:
  A: $y=n x+b$
  B: $y=n x-b$
  C: $y=b(n)^{x}$
  D: $y=n(b)^{x}$

  B: 0 and 4
  C: -4 and 4
  D: 4

  Check if the solution satisfies the original equation.
  
Action: Answer("B")

  $$2x(x-3)=2(x-3)x$$
  $$2x^2-6x=2x^2-6x$$
  $$0=0$$
  The equation is true for all values of $x$ except $x=0$ and $x=3$ since they make the denominator zero.
  Plugging in $x=0$ and $x=3$ into the original equation, we get undefined expressions.
  Therefore, the possible values of $x$ that satisfy the equation are $0$ and $4$.

  A: $\frac{12}{5}$
  B: $\frac{16}{7}$
  C: $-\frac{16}{7}$
  D: $-\frac{12}{5}$

  For the two lines to be parallel, their slopes must be equal.
  Therefore, we need to solve the equation $\frac{k}{3}=\frac{4}{5}$ for $k$.
  Solving for $k$, we get $k=\frac{12}{5}\neq\frac{16}{7},-\frac{16}{7},-\frac{12}{5}$.
  Therefore, the answer is A: $\frac{12}{5}$.

### Temperature: 3.0 | Problem 100 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: If $\frac{2 a}{b}=\frac{1}{2}$, what is the value of $\frac{b}{a} ?$
Choices:
  A: $\frac{1}{8}$
  B: $\frac{1}{4}$
  C: 2
  D: 4
Response 0:
Thought:
  We can solve for $\frac{b}{a}$ by isolating it on one side of the equation.
  Multiply both sides by $\frac{b}{2}$ to get rid of the fraction on the left side.
  Simplify the right side.
  Divide both sides by $2a$ to isolate $\frac{b}{a}$.
  The answer is $\frac{b}{a} = \frac{1}{4}$.
Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Thought:
  We can solve for $\frac{b}{a}$ by isolating it on one side of the equation.
  Multiply both sides of the equation by $\frac{b}{2}$ to get rid of the fraction.
  $\frac{2a}{b} \cdot \frac{b}{2} = \frac{1}{2} \cdot \frac{b}{2}$
  Simplify the left side of the equation.
  $a = \frac{b}{4}$
  Divide both sides of the equation by $a$ to solve for $\frac{b}{a}$.
  $\frac{a}{a} = \frac{b/4}{a}$
  Simplify the right side of the equation.
  $\frac{b}{4a}$
  Therefore, $\frac{b}{a} = \frac{b}{4a} \cdot 4 = \frac{4b}{4a} = \frac{b}{a} = \boxed{\textbf{(C) }2}$
Action: Answer("C")
Response 2:
Thought:
  We can start by cross-multiplying the given equation to get rid of the fraction.
  $\frac{2 a}{b}=\frac{1}{2} \Rightarrow 2a = \frac{b}{2} \Rightarrow 2a = \frac{1}{2}b$
  We can then solve for $\frac{b}{a}$ by dividing both sides by $a$.
  $2a = \frac{1}{2}b \Rightarrow \frac{b}{a} = \frac{2a}{a} \div \frac{1}{2} \Rightarrow \frac{b}{a} = 4$
  Therefore, the answer is D: 4.
Action: Answer("D")
Response 3:
Thought:
  We can solve for $\frac{b}{a}$ using the given equation.
  Multiply both sides of the equation by $\frac{b}{2}$ to isolate $\frac{b}{a}$.
  $\frac{2 a}{b}=\frac{1}{2}$
  $\frac{2 a}{b} \cdot \frac{b}{2}=\frac{1}{2} \cdot \frac{b}{2}$
  $a=\frac{b}{4}$
  $\frac{b}{a}=\frac{b}{\frac{b}{4}}=4$
  Therefore, the value of $\frac{b}{a}$ is 4.
  The answer is D: 4.
